   recipe Make Male Wig

	LeatherStrips=5,
	PaintWhite/HairDyeWhite=1,

        Result:Wigs_MHairMullet_White,
        Time:55.0,
	SkillRequired:Tailoring=10,
        Category:Wigs,
    }
